const DATA\+\_\+\+URL\+\_\+\+PATTERN = /\texorpdfstring{$^\wedge$}{\string^}data\+:(?\+:image\textbackslash{}/(?\+:bmp\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}gif\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}jpeg\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}jpg\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}png\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}tiff\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}webp)\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}video\textbackslash{}/(?\+:mpeg\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}mp4\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}ogg\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}webm)\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}audio\textbackslash{}/(?\+:mp3\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}oga\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}ogg\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}opus))}



A pattern that matches safe data URLs. 

Only matches image, video and audio types.
